country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3
	title = play_as_ruler.3.name
	picture = GFX_evt_throne_room
	desc = { #FirstTime
		trigger = { 
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3.desc_01
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = "play_as_ruler_firsttime_end"			
				}
			}
			text = "newline"
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3.desc_endline_firsttime
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = "play_as_ruler_firsttime_end"			
				}
			}
		}
	}

#Second Time and Later
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			text = play_as_ruler.3.desc_02
			success_text = {
				text = "newline"
				has_country_flag = "play_as_ruler_talk_nothing"
				has_country_flag = "play_as_ruler_firsttime_end"			
			}
			text = play_as_ruler.3.desc_endline
		}
	}

	option = {
#		name = play_as_ruler.3.b
		name = yaya_research_focus
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_research_focus
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = ruler_research_focus_1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5		
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				minerals < 1000
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				energy < 1000
			}				
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.4 }
		}
		add_modifier = {
				modifier = ruler_research_focus_1
				days = 3600
			}
		add_influence = -100
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_research_focus
	}

	option = {
#		name = play_as_ruler.3.c
		name = yaya_mineral_focus
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_minerals_focus
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = ruler_energy_focus_1
				has_modifier = ruler_minerals_focus_1
				has_modifier = ruler_industrial_focus_1
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_ethic = ethic_industrial
						has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_industrial
					}
					has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ethic_industrial
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				minerals < 2000
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				energy < 1000
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.4 }
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = ruler_minerals_focus_1
			days = 3600
		}
		add_influence = -100
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_minerals_focus
	}

	option = {
		name = yaya_industrial_focus
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ethic_industrial
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_industrial
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_industrial
			}
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = ruler_energy_focus_1
				has_modifier = ruler_minerals_focus_1
				has_modifier = ruler_capitalism_focus_1
				has_modifier = ruler_industrial_focus_1	
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_industrial
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_industrial
				}
			}									
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.4 }
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = ruler_industrial_focus_1
			days = 3600
		}
		add_influence = -115
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ethic_industrial
	}

			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ship_combat_focus
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ship_combat_focus_improve
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = ruler_ship_combat_focus_1
				has_modifier = ruler_ship_combat_focus_2
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ship_combat_focus_improve				
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality = democratic_crusaders
					has_ai_personality = hegemonic_imperialists	
					has_ai_personality = ruthless_capitalists	
					has_ai_personality = fanatic_purifiers	
					has_ai_personality = metalhead
					
				}
			}		
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_militarist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
				}
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				minerals < 1000
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				energy < 1000
			}					
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.4 }
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = ruler_ship_combat_focus_2
			days = 3600
		}
		add_influence = -100
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ship_combat_focus
	}

		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_colonize_focus
	}
	after = {
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_random_talk_01
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_random_talk_02
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_random_talk_03
	}
}

###IF YOUR EMPIRE HAS ♂PHILOSOPHER KING♂ CIVIC###
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.20
	title = play_as_ruler.20.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.20.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_alien_propaganda
	show_sound = event_heir_new
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		any_owned_leader = {
			OR = {
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv1
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv2
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv3
			}
			NOT = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_is_philosopher_king
			}
		}
		has_civic = civic_philosopher_king
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = { 
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			save_event_target_as = ruler
			set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_is_philosopher_king
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv1
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv2
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv3
					}
				}
				remove_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv1 
				remove_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv2
				remove_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv3
				add_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv4
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.20.a
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv4
			}	
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = influence
			value = 12
			min = 75
			max = 150
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 6
			min = 125
			max = 2000
		}
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.20.tooltip
	}
}
###RULER SHIP AND STATION###
#YOU NEED A MOD THAT ADD RULER SHIP AND STATION FOR THIS WORKS#
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.30
	title = play_as_ruler.30.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.30.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_alien_propaganda
	show_sound = event_10_exp
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			has_leader_flag = built_ruler_ship
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_built_ruler_ship
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_authority = auth_imperial
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = play_as_ruler_ruler_ship_cooldown
				days = 3599
			}
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.31 days = 3600 } 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_authority = auth_dictatorial
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = play_as_ruler_ruler_ship_cooldown
				days = 5399
			}
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.31 days = 5400 } 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_authority = auth_imperial
					has_authority = auth_dictatorial				
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = play_as_ruler_ruler_ship_cooldown
				days = 7199
			}
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.31 days = 7200 } 
		}
		set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_built_ruler_ship #SO PLAYER CAN'T USE CANCEL SPAMMING TRICK TO SPAM RULER SHIP
	}
}
###REMOVE THE FLAG AND CALL IT A DAY LOL###
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.31
	title = play_as_ruler.31.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.31.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hangar_bay
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	hide_window = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_built_ruler_ship
		NOT = {
			has_modifier = play_as_ruler_ruler_ship_cooldown
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
				has_leader_flag = built_ruler_ship
			}
			remove_leader_flag = built_ruler_ship
			save_event_target_as = ruler
		}
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_built_ruler_ship
	}
	option = {
		name = OK
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.31.tooltip
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.36
	title = play_as_ruler.36.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.36.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_interior_battle
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_built_ruler_ship
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_built_ruler_station
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_built_ruler_army
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = built_ruler_ship
					}
					ROOT = {
						has_modifier = play_as_ruler_ruler_ship_cooldown
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					remove_modifier = play_as_ruler_ruler_ship_cooldown		
					remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_built_ruler_ship					
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = has_built_station
					}
					ROOT = {
						has_modifier = play_as_ruler_ruler_station_cooldown
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					remove_modifier = play_as_ruler_ruler_station_cooldown	
					remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_built_ruler_station					
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = has_elite_guard
					}
					ROOT = {
						has_modifier = play_as_ruler_ruler_army_cooldown
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					remove_modifier = play_as_ruler_ruler_army_cooldown
					remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_built_ruler_army					
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
###CAMPAIGN IMPROVE###
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.50
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_exp value > 750 }
		OR = {
			has_modifier = ruler_build_focus_1
			has_modifier = ruler_clean_tile_focus_1
			has_modifier = ruler_ftl_focus_1
			has_modifier = ruler_ship_build_focus_1
			has_modifier = ruler_ship_cost_focus_1
			has_modifier = ruler_ship_combat_focus_1
			has_modifier = ruler_ship_power_focus_1
			has_modifier = ruler_trade_focus_1
			has_modifier = ruler_trust_focus_1
			has_modifier = ruler_survey_focus_1
			has_modifier = ruler_speed_focus_1
			has_modifier = ruler_colonize_focus_1
			has_modifier = ruler_happy_focus_1
			has_modifier = ruler_edict_focus_1
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 15
	}
	
	immediate = {
		subtract_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_exp value = 750 }
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_modifier = ruler_build_focus_1
				NOT = { has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_build_focus_improve }
			}
			set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_build_focus_improve
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.51 }
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_modifier = ruler_clean_tile_focus_1
				NOT = { has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_clean_tile_focus_improve }
			}
			set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_clean_tile_focus_improve
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.52 }
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = ruler_ftl_focus_1 
				NOT = { has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ftl_focus_improve }
			}
			set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ftl_focus_improve
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.53 }
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_modifier = ruler_ship_build_focus_1
				NOT = { has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ship_build_focus_improve }
			}
			set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ship_build_focus_improve

			set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ship_cost_focus_improve
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.55 }
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_modifier = ruler_ship_combat_focus_1 
				NOT = { has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ship_combat_focus_improve }
			}
			set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ship_combat_focus_improve
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.56 }
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_modifier = ruler_ship_power_focus_1 
				NOT = { has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ship_power_focus_improve }
			}
			set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_ship_power_focus_improve
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.57 }
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

				NOT = { has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_trade_focus_improve }
			}
			set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_trade_focus_improve
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.58 }
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_modifier = ruler_trust_focus_1
				NOT = { has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_trust_focus_improve }
			}
			set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_trust_focus_improve
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.59 }
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9100 }

###RULER EXP REACHED 10, GIVE GIVE!###
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.8993
	picture = GFX_evt_archaeological_dig
	show_sound = event_celebration
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value > 9 }
		}
		NOT = {
			has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			subtract_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 10 }
			save_event_target_as = ruler
		}
		random_list = {
			1 = { set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_energy }
			1 = { set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_minerals }
			1 = { set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_unity }
		}
		random_list = {
			1 = { set_timed_country_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_1 days = 20 } }
			1 = { set_timed_country_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_2 days = 20 } }
			1 = { set_timed_country_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_3 days = 20 } }
		}
		country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.8994 days = 1 }
	}	
}
#EXP 15#
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.8994
    title = play_as_ruler.8994.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.8994.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_alien_propaganda
	show_sound = event_10_exp
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
		}	
	}

	immediate = {
	}	
	option = {
		name = OK
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_1
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_2
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_3
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = SPLENDID
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = GOOD
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_3
		}
	}
	after = {
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = influence
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 40
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_energy
				NOT = {
					event_target:ruler = {
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_synthetic
					}
				}
			}
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = energy
				value = 3
				min = 125
				max = 500
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_minerals
			}
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = minerals
				value = 3
				min = 125
				max = 500
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_unity
				NOT = {
					event_target:ruler = {
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
					}			
				}
			}
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = 3
				min = 125
				max = 750
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_unity
				event_target:ruler = {
					has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
				}
			}
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = 3
				min = 125
				max = 1000
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_energy
				event_target:ruler = {
					has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_synthetic
				}
			}
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = energy
				value = 3
				min = 150
				max = 750
			}
		}
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_energy
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_minerals
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_exp_10_unity
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.8995
	picture = GFX_evt_archaeological_dig
	show_sound = event_celebration
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value > 35 }
		}	
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			divide_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 2 }
		}
	}	
}
#####+1 RULED TIME TO COUNTRY#####
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.8996
	picture = GFX_evt_archaeological_dig
	show_sound = event_celebration
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_ruled_time value > 0 }
		}	
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ROOT = {
			change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_ruled_time_country value = 1 }
		}
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			subtract_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_ruled_time value = 1 }
		}
	}	
}

#play_as_ruler_exp = Ruler exp for their life time, +1 every year ( affected by campaign )
#once reached 20 will gain gift from ppl then -20 their exp
#play_as_ruler_hobby_exp = Ruler hobby exp for every hobby finish, +10
#hobby enhanced event will happen when they have 30 or more
#play_as_ruler_campaign_exp = will incresed each year every campaign they hold,
#used to unlock handy policy or ethics like +1s +1s stuff like that (at least 250+)
#9010 = hobby starter, 9020 = hobby remover, 3000~4500 = hobby events
#9100 = hivemind placeholder 9200 = ruler level bar on right 9499 = Hobby select informer

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.9001
	title = play_as_ruler.9001.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.9001.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_alien_propaganda
	show_sound = event_celebration
#	is_triggered_only = yes
	auto_opens = no

	trigger = {
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv1
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
		}	
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_levelup_cooldown
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 720
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_ruled_time_country value > 5 }
		}

	}	
	
	immediate = {
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler_levelup_cooldown days = 180 }	
	hidden_effect = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv1
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			add_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv2
			remove_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv1
		}		
	}
	}
	
	after = {

	}
	
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.9000.a
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 350
		}
	}
}

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2400
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_ruled_time_country value > 15 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			has_civic = civic_philosopher_king
			NOT = {
				has_invalid_civic = civic_philosopher_king
			}
		}
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler_levelup_cooldown days = 180 }	
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_leader = {
				limit = {
					leader_class = ruler
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv3
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
				}
				add_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv4
				remove_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv3
			}
		}		
	}
	
	after = {

	}

		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 5

			max = 600
		}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.9010
#	title = play_as_ruler.gethobby
#	desc = play_as_ruler.9010.desc
#	picture = GFX_evt_archaeological_dig
#	show_sound = event_celebration
#	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {	
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_hive_mind
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_ecomony
				}
				random_list = {
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9011 } }#Agrarian 	
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9012 } }#Constructor
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9022 } }#Social Research
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9024 } }#Resource Recycle		
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_product
				}
				random_list = {
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9014 } }#Credit Investor	
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9012 } }#Constructor
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9016 } }#Miner
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9023 } }#Engineering Research
				}					
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_influence
				}
				random_list = {
					3 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9018 } }#Gaining Influence
					3 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9019 } }#Flavor Edicts
					3 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9025 } }#Power Unity	
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_research
				}
				random_list = {
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9017 } }#Researcher
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9021 } }#Physics Research
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9022 } }#Social Research
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9023 } }#Engineering Research
				}					
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_research
				}
				random_list = {
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9017 } }#Researcher
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9021 } }#Physics Research
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9022 } }#Social Research
					2 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9023 } }#Engineering Research		
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_ship
				}
				random_list = {
					3 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9013 } }#Ship Builder
					3 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9021 } }#Physics Research
					3 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9015 } }#Logistician
				}				
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_random_choose
				}
				country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9500 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.9499
	title = play_as_ruler.9499.name
#	desc = play_as_ruler.9499.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_throne_room
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
#	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.9499.desc
				has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_random_choose
			} 
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.9499.desc_hive
				has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_hive_placeholder
			} 
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.9499.desc_machine
				has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_machine_placeholder
			} 
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_random_choose
			has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_hive_placeholder
			has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_machine_placeholder
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_choose_hobby_noticer
		} 
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 20
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_choose_hobby_noticer
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			save_event_target_as = ruler
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.9499.a
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.9499.tooltip
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.9200
#	title = play_as_ruler.gethobby
#	desc = play_as_ruler.9200.desc
#	picture = GFX_evt_archaeological_dig
#	show_sound = event_celebration
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {	
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_hive_mind
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv1
				}
				remove_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv1
				add_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv1

	trigger = {

			has_country_flag = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_cooldown
		}
		leader = {
			leader_class = ruler					
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			NOR = {
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_builder
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_fleet
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_miner
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_influence
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_builder_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_fleet_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_miner_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_influence_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_builder_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_fleet_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_miner_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_influence_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine
			}
		}
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 10
#	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_agrarian_3
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_experted
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_expert
				root = {
					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_agrarian_2
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_experted
					}
				}
				Hidden_effect = {
					FROM = {
						country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9031 days = 360 random = 360 }
					}
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_agrarian_1
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_agrarian_3
					}
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_experienced
				set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_agrarian_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_agrarian_1
					}
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian
				set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_agrarian_1
			}
			root = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv5
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv6
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv7
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv8
					}
				}
				root = {
#					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv9
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv10
					}
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					root = {
						check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value > 5 }
					}
				}
				root = {
					set_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_hobby_longer
				}
				country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9020 days = 3600 random = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_hobby_longer
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9020 days = 1800 random = 0 }
			}
		}
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_cooldown days = 5400 }		
	}
	option = {
		name = OK
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = GOOD
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_experienced
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_expert
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9200 }
		}
	}
	
}

				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_builder_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_fleet_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_miner_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_influence_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_builder_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_fleet_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_miner_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_influence_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine
			}
		}
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 10
#	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_investor_3
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_experted
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_expert
				root = {
					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_investor_2
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_experted
					}
				}
				Hidden_effect = {
					FROM = {
						country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9034 days = 360 random = 360 }
					}
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_investor_1
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_investor_3
					}
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_experienced
				set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_investor_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_investor_1
					}
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor
				set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_investor_1
			}
			root = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv5
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv6
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv7
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv8
					}
				}
				root = {
#					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv9
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv10
					}
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					root = {
						check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value > 5 }
					}
				}
				root = {
					set_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_hobby_longer
				}
				country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9020 days = 3600 random = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_hobby_longer
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9020 days = 1800 random = 0 }
			}
		}	
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_cooldown days = 5400 }		
	}
	option = {
		name = OK
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = GOOD
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_experienced
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_expert
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9200 }
		}
	}
}

				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_builder_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_fleet_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_miner_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_influence_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine
			}
		}
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 10
#	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_research_3
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_experted
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_expert
				root = {
					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_research_2
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_experted
					}
				}
				Hidden_effect = {
					FROM = {
						country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9037 days = 360 random = 360 }
					}
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_research_1
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_research_3
					}
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_experienced
				set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_research_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_research_1
					}
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research
				set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_research_1
			}
			root = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv5
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv6
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv7
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv8
					}
				}
				root = {
#					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv9
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv10
					}
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					root = {
						check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value > 5 }
					}
				}
				root = {
					set_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_hobby_longer
				}
				country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9020 days = 3600 random = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_hobby_longer
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9020 days = 1800 random = 0 }
			}
		}
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = trait_ruler_hobby_research_cooldown days = 5400 }		
	}
	option = {
		name = OK
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = GOOD
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_experienced
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_expert
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9200 }
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_physic_3
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_experted
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_expert
				root = {
					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_physic_2
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_experted
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					FROM = {
						country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9038 days = 360 random = 360 }
					}
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_physic_1
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_physic_3
					}
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_experienced
				set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_physic_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_physic_1
					}
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic
				set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_physic_1
			}
			root = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv5
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv6
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv7
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv8
					}
				}
				root = {
#					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv9
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv10
					}
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					root = {
						check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value > 5 }
					}
				}
				root = {
					set_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_hobby_longer
				}
				country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9020 days = 3600 random = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_hobby_longer
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9020 days = 1800 random = 0 }
			}
		}	
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_cooldown days = 5400 }
	}
	option = {
		name = OK
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = GOOD
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_experienced
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_expert
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9200 }
		}
	}
}

					}
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle_experienced
				set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_recycle_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_recycle_1
					}
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle
				set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_recycle_1
			}
			root = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv5
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv6
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv7
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv8
					}
				}
				root = {
#					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv9
						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv10
					}
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					root = {
						check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value > 5 }
					}
				}
				root = {
					set_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_hobby_longer
				}
				country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9020 days = 3600 random = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_hobby_longer
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9020 days = 1800 random = 0 }
			}
		}	
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle_cooldown days = 5400 }
	}
	option = {
		name = OK
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = GOOD
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle_experienced
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle_expert
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = trait_ruler_hobby_tooltip
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9200 }
		}
	}
}

	auto_opens = no

	trigger = {	
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = trait_ruler_hobby_unity_cooldown
		}
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler			
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			NOR = {

				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_fleet
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_miner
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_influence
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_builder_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_fleet_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_miner_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_influence_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_builder_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_fleet_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_miner_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_influence_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine
			}
		}
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 10
#	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_unity_3
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_experted
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity_expert
				root = {
					change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_amount value = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_unity_2
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_experted
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					FROM = {
						country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.9044 days = 360 random = 360 }
					}
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_unity_1
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_unity_3
					}
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity_experienced
				set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_unity_2
			}
			if = {

						has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv7

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.9100

	picture = GFX_evt_archaeological_dig
#	show_sound = event_administrative_work
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {	
		OR = {
			has_authority = auth_hive_mind
			has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
			has_authority = auth_ancient_machine_intelligence
			has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
		}
		
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			OR = {
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv1
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv2
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv3
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv4
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv5
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv6
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv7
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv8
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv9
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv10
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine
			}
		}
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 10
#	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = { 
				leader_class = ruler
				OR = {
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv1
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv2
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv3
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv4
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv5
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv6
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv7
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv8
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv9
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv10
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive
					has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						has_authority = auth_hive_mind
					}
					NOT = {
						has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive
					}
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
							has_authority = auth_ancient_machine_intelligence					
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine
					}
				}
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine
			}			
		}	
		set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_hive_mind
	}
}

				remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive_research
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive_growth
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_policy_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_focus_hive_ecomony
			}
			random_owned_leader = {
				limit = {

				remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive_ecomony
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive_military
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive_influence
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive_research
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_hive_ecomony
			}

					leader_class = ruler
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
					NOT = {
						has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine_research
					}
				}
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine_ecomony
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine_military
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine_influence
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine_research
				add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_machine_research
			}
		}
	}
}


###HOBBY REMOVER###
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.9020
	title = play_as_ruler.9020.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.9020.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_archaeological_dig
#	show_sound = event_celebration
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {	
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			NOT = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_elected
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = { 
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_builder
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_fleet
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_miner
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_influence
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_builder_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_fleet_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_miner_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_influence_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity_experienced
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_expert
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_builder_expert
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_fleet_expert
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_expert
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_expert
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_miner_expert
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_expert
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_influence_expert
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict_expert
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_expert
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social_expert
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering_expert
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_recycle_expert
			remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_unity_expert
			change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
					has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
				}
				remove_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
			}
		}	
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_meme
		random_list = {
			90 = {}
			10 = { set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_meme }
		}
	}
}

###RULER WANT TO EXPERTIZE THEIR OWN HOBBY###
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.9031
	title = play_as_ruler.consider_expert
#	desc = play_as_ruler.9031.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_argrian
	show_sound = event_character_event
	is_triggered_only = yes

	desc = { #FirstTime
		trigger = { 
			text = "play_as_ruler.9031.desc"
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.consider_firsttime
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = "play_as_ruler_hobby_expert_firsttime"			
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = { #After
		trigger = { 
			success_text = {
				text = "play_as_ruler.9031.desc"
				has_country_flag = "play_as_ruler_hobby_expert_firsttime"
			}
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {	
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler			
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_agrarian_2
			has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_experienced
			NOR = {
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_experted
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			save_event_target_as = ruler
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.consider_yes
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_experienced
			}		
		}
		event_target:ruler = {
			add_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_expert
			set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_experted
			set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_agrarian_3
		}
		custom_tooltip = ruler_consider_yes_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_experienced
			}	
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.consider_no
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_meme
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.consider_no_meme
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_meme
		}
		custom_tooltip = ruler_consider_tooltip
	}
	after = {
		set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_expert_firsttime		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.2998
	title = play_as_ruler.2998.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.2998.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_alien_propaganda
	show_sound = event_character_event
#	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {	
		has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_has_hobby_event
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler			
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value > 10 }
			NOT = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_cooldown
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.2999_event_cooldown
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1080
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			effect_play_as_ruler_hobby_event_ended = yes
		}
		random_list = {
			1 = { set_timed_country_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_reward_good days = 2 } }
			1 = { set_timed_country_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_reward_normal days = 2 } }
			1 = { set_timed_country_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_reward_bad days = 2 } }
		}
		event_target:ruler = {
			set_timed_leader_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler.2999_event_cooldown days = 3600 }
		}
	}
	after = {
		country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.2999 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.2999
	title = play_as_ruler.hobby.reward.name

	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	is_triggered_only = yes

	desc = { #GOOD
		trigger = { 
			success_text = {
				text = "play_as_ruler.2999.desc.good"
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_reward_good
			}
		}
	}

	desc = { #NORMAL
		trigger = {

		}
	}

	desc = { #BAD

			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.hobby.reward.good_01
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_reward_good
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_random_talk_01
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value = 10 }
			}	
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = influence
			value = 3
			min = 10
			max = 25
		}
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.hobby.exp.increase.tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.hobby.reward.good_02

			}	
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = influence
			value = 3
			min = 10
			max = 25
		}
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.hobby.exp.increase.tooltip
	}
	option = {

			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_random_talk_03
		}

			resource = influence
			value = 3
			min = 10
			max = 25
		}

	}
	option = {

		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_reward_normal		
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value = 5 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.hobby.exp.increase.tooltip
	}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3000
	title = play_as_ruler.3000.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3000.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_argrian
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
#	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {	
		has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_has_hobby_event
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler			
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			or = {
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_expert
			}
			check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value > 15 }
			NOT = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_cooldown
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.3000_event_cooldown
			}
		}
		any_controlled_planet = {
			num_pops > 1
			num_pops < 6
			is_capital = no
			is_homeworld = no
			has_ground_combat = no
			NOT = {
				has_planet_flag = play_as_ruler_agrarian_planet_event1
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1080
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			effect_play_as_ruler_hobby_event_ended = yes
		}
		random_controlled_planet = { 
			limit = {
				num_pops > 1
				num_pops < 6
				is_capital = no
				is_homeworld = no
				has_ground_combat = no
				NOT = {
					has_planet_flag = play_as_ruler_agrarian_planet_event1
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = planet
			set_planet_flag = play_as_ruler_agrarian_planet_event1
		}
		random_controlled_planet = { 
			limit = {
				is_homeworld = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = homeplanet
		}
		random_controlled_planet = { 
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = capitalplanet
		}
		event_target:ruler = {
			set_timed_leader_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler.3000_event_cooldown days = 3600 }
		}
		country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3001 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3001
	title = play_as_ruler.3000.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3001.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_argrian
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes
	location = event_target:planet

	trigger = {	
	}

	
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3001.a
		trigger = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value > 30 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3002 days = 10 random = 10 }
			event_target:ruler = {
				subtract_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value = 15 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.hobby.exp.highenough.tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3001.b
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				OR = {
					has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_experienced
					has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_agrarian_expert				
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3004 days = 10 random = 10 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3001.c
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3002 days = 10 random = 10 } }
				50 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3003 days = 10 random = 10 } }
			}
		}
		print_scope_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3001.d
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3004 days = 10 random = 10 } }
				50 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3005 days = 10 random = 10 } }
			}
		}
		print_scope_effect = yes
	}
	after = {
	}
}

	id = play_as_ruler.3002
	title = play_as_ruler.3002.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3002.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_metropolis
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes
	location = event_target:capitalplanet

	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.hobby.reward.good_01
		event_target:planet = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = ruler_planet_agrarian_good1
				days = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 1 }
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = influence
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 40
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 350
		}
	}
}

	show_sound = event_planetary_riot
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes
	location = event_target:planet

	immediate = {
		event_target:planet = {
			random_tile = {
				limit = { 
					has_building = yes
					is_ruined = no
					NOT = { 
						has_building = "building_colony_shelter"
						has_building = "building_capital_1"
						has_building = "building_capital_2"
						has_building = "building_capital_3"
					}
				}
				set_ruined = yes #remove_building = yes
			}
			random_pop = {
				limit = {
					event_target:planet = {
						num_pops > 2
					}
				}
				kill_pop = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3005.a
		event_target:planet = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = ruler_planet_agrarian_bad2
				days = 3600
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				subtract_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value = 15 }
			}
		}
		add_influence = -25
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.hobby.exp.decrease.tooltip
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3103
	title = play_as_ruler.3103.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3103.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_metropolis
	show_sound = event_planetary_riot
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes
	location = event_target:planet

	immediate = {
		every_owned_planet = {
			limit = {
				has_planet_flag = play_as_ruler_miner_planet_event1
			}
			random_tile = {
				limit = { 
					has_building = yes
					is_ruined = no
					NOT = { 
						has_building = "building_colony_shelter"
						has_building = "building_capital_1"
						has_building = "building_capital_2"
						has_building = "building_capital_3"
					}
				}
				set_ruined = yes #remove_building = yes
			}
			random_tile = {
				limit = { 
					has_building = yes
					is_ruined = no
					NOT = { 
						has_building = "building_colony_shelter"
						has_building = "building_capital_1"
						has_building = "building_capital_2"
						has_building = "building_capital_3"
					}
				}
				set_ruined = yes #remove_building = yes
			}
			random_tile = {
				limit = { 
					event_target:planet = {
						num_pops > 5
					}
					has_building = yes
					is_ruined = no
					NOT = { 
						has_building = "building_colony_shelter"
						has_building = "building_capital_1"
						has_building = "building_capital_2"

					}
				}
				set_ruined = yes #remove_building = yes
			}

						num_pops > 10
					}

					is_ruined = no
					NOT = {

		name = UNFORTUNATE

			limit = {

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3105
	title = play_as_ruler.3105.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3105.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_miner
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes
	location = event_target:planet

	trigger = {	
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 1080
#	}

	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.hobby.reward.good_01
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 1 }
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = minerals
			value = 3
			min = 250
			max = 1000
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = influence
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 40
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 350
		}
		event_target:planet = {
			remove_planet_flag = play_as_ruler_miner_planet_event1
		}
	}
}

#INTERESTING ROCKS

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3107
	title = play_as_ruler.3107.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3107.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_miner
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes
	location = event_target:planet

	trigger = {	
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 1080
#	}

	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3107.a
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value = 5 }
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 1 }
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = influence
			value = 12
			min = 50
			max = 150
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 350
		}
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.hobby.exp.increase.tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3107.b
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value = 5 }
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 1 }
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = energy
			value = 6
			min = 200
			max = 1250
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 350
		}
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.hobby.exp.increase.tooltip
		every_owned_planet = {
			limit = {
				has_planet_flag = play_as_ruler_miner_planet_event1
			}
			remove_planet_flag = play_as_ruler_miner_planet_event1
		}
	}
}

#Logistician
#YO ONE OF DE ADMIRER IS STEALING YOUR GOOD, SHOULDN'T YOU NOSCOPE THAT SCRUB?
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3200
	title = play_as_ruler.3200.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3200.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_logistician
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
#	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {	
		has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_has_hobby_event
		minerals > 500
		energy > 500
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = admiral
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = leader_trait_cautious
					has_trait = leader_trait_fleet_logistician
				}
			}
		}
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			or = {
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_experienced		
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_expert
			}
			check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value > 15 }
			NOT = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_cooldown
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.3200_event_cooldown
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1080
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			effect_play_as_ruler_hobby_event_ended = yes
		}
		random_owned_leader = { 
			limit = {
				leader_class = admiral
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = leader_trait_cautious
						has_trait = leader_trait_fleet_logistician
					}
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = admiral
			set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_admiral_stolen
		}
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			set_timed_leader_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler.3200_event_cooldown days = 3600 }
		}
		every_owned_leader = { 
			limit = {
#				leader_class = admiral
				NOT = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_admiral_stolen	
				}			
			}
			set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_not_admiral_stolen
		}
		add_energy = -250
		add_minerals = -250
		if = {
			limit = {
				minerals > 2500
			}
			add_minerals = -2500
			set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_stolen_minerals
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				energy > 2500
			}
			add_energy = -2500
			set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_stolen_energy
		}
		country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3201 days = 3 random = 4 }
	}
	after = {
	}
}

#START SEARCHING M8
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3201
	title = play_as_ruler.3200.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3201.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_logistician
	show_sound = event_administrative_work
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes
#	location = event_target:admiral

	trigger = {	
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 1080
#	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = { 
			limit = {
				leader_class = admiral
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_admiral_stolen			
			}
			save_event_target_as = admiral
		}
		random_owned_leader = { 
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself			
			}
			save_event_target_as = ruler
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3201.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3202 days = 20 random = 10 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.3201.tooltip
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3205 days = 130 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3202
	title = play_as_ruler.3202.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3202.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_logistician
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes
#	location = event_target:admiral

	trigger = {	
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = admiral
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_admiral_stolen
		}
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 1080
#	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = { 
			limit = {
				leader_class = admiral
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_admiral_stolen			
			}
			save_event_target_as = admiral
		}
		random_owned_leader = { 
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself			
			}
			save_event_target_as = ruler
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3202.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3203 days = 20 random = 10 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3202.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_meme
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:admiral = {
				exile_leader_as = admiral
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.3202.tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3202.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_meme
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:admiral = {
				exile_leader_as = admiral
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.3202.meme
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3205 days = 100 }
		}
	}
}

#GOT HIM
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3203
	title = play_as_ruler.3203.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3203.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_logistician
	show_sound = event_conversation
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes
#	location = event_target:admiral

	trigger = {	
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = admiral
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_admiral_stolen
		}
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 1080
#	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = { 
			limit = {
				leader_class = admiral
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_admiral_stolen			
			}
			save_event_target_as = admiral
		}
		random_owned_leader = { 
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself			
			}
			save_event_target_as = ruler
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3203.a
		trigger = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value > 30 }
				NOT = {
					has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_experienced
					has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_expert
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3204 days = 30 random = 30 }
			subtract_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value = 15 }
		}
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler.3204.good days = 60 }
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.hobby.exp.highenough.tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3203.a
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				or = {
					has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_experienced
					has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_logistician_expert
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3204 days = 30 random = 30 }
		}
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler.3204.good days = 60 }
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3203.b
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3204 days = 30 random = 30 }
			random_list = {
				50 = { set_timed_country_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler.3204.ok days = 60 } }
				50 = { set_timed_country_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler.3204.bad days = 60 } }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3203.c
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:admiral = {
				exile_leader_as = admiral
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.3203.c.tooltip
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3205 days = 70 }
		}
	}
}

#LETS SEE WHAT HE GOT
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3204
	title = play_as_ruler.3204.name
#	desc = play_as_ruler.3204.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_logistician
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes
#	location = event_target:admiral

	desc = {
		trigger = { 
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3204.desc_01
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3204.good
			}
		}	
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = { 
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3204.desc_02
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3204.ok
			}
		}	
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = { 
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3204.desc_03
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3204.bad
			}
		}	
	}
	
	trigger = {	
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = admiral
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_admiral_stolen
		}
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 1080
#	}
	
	immediate = {
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_stolen_energy
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_stolen_minerals	
		event_target:admiral = {
			remove_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_admiral_stolen
		}
		every_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_not_admiral_stolen
			}
			remove_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_not_admiral_stolen
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3204.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3204.good
		}
		event_target:admiral = {
			add_experience = 400
			add_trait = leader_trait_fleet_logistician
			add_trait = leader_trait_cautious
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = leader_trait_lethargic
				}
				remove_trait = leader_trait_lethargic
			}
			
		}
		add_energy = 250
		add_minerals = 250
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_stolen_energy
			}
			add_energy = 1500
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_stolen_minerals
			}
			add_minerals = 1500
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = influence
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 40
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 350
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3204.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3204.ok
		}
		add_energy = 250
		add_minerals = 250
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_stolen_energy
			}
			add_energy = 1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_stolen_minerals
			}
			add_minerals = 1000
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = influence
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 40
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 350
		}
		event_target:admiral = {
			add_experience = 200
			add_trait = leader_trait_fleet_logistician
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3204.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3204.bad
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				subtract_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value = 5 }
			}
		}
		add_influence = -25
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.hobby.exp.decrease.tooltip
	}
	
	after = {

	}
	
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3205
	title = play_as_ruler.3205.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3205.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_logistician
	show_sound = event_ship_thrusters
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {	
		any_owned_leader = {
			NOT = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_admiral_stolen
			}
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_not_admiral_stolen
		}
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 1080
#	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
#				leader_class = admiral
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_not_admiral_stolen
			}
			remove_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_not_admiral_stolen
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = GOOD
		add_energy = 250
		add_minerals = 250
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_stolen_energy
			}
			add_energy = 2500
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_stolen_minerals
			}
			add_minerals = 2500
		}
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_stolen_energy
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_logistician_stolen_minerals
	}
}
