country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3300
	title = play_as_ruler.3300.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3300.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_galactic_senate
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
#	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	location = event_target:planet

	trigger = {	
		has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_has_hobby_event
		influence > 100
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler			
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			or = {
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict_experienced		
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict_expert
			}
			check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value > 15 }
			NOT = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_cooldown
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.3300_event_cooldown
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1080
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			effect_play_as_ruler_hobby_event_ended = yes
		}
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			set_timed_leader_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler.3300_event_cooldown days = 3600 }
		}
		random_owned_planet = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = planet
		}
		country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3301 }
	}
	after = {
	}
}

#NOT YET BUDDY, P L S WAIT
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3301
	title = play_as_ruler.3300.name
#	desc = play_as_ruler.3301.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_medieval_alien_civilization
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes
	location = event_target:planet

	desc = {
		trigger = { 
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3301.desc
				event_target:ruler = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
							has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}	
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = { 
			success_text = {

#	}

			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			save_event_target_as = ruler
		}
		random_owned_planet = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = planet
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3301.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				event_target:ruler = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_influence = -50
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3302 days = 20 random = 40 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3301.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				event_target:ruler = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3304
	title = play_as_ruler.3304.name
#	desc = play_as_ruler.3304.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_medieval_alien_civilization
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes
	location = event_target:planet

	desc = {
		trigger = { 
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3304.desc_01
				event_target:ruler = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
					}
				}
			}
			text = "newline"
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3304.desc_psionic_01
				event_target:ruler = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
					}
				}
			}
			text = "newline"
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3304.desc_psionic_02
				event_target:ruler = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
					}
				}
			}
		}	
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = { 
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3304.desc_01
				event_target:ruler = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
							has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
						}
					}
				}
			}
			text = "newline"
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3304.desc_02
				event_target:ruler = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
							has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
						}
					}
				}
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3304.success
			}
		}	
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = { 
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3304.desc_01
				event_target:ruler = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
							has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
						}
					}
				}
			}
			text = "newline"
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3304.desc_03
				event_target:ruler = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
							has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3304.success				
				}
			}
		}	
	}

	trigger = {	
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 1080
#	}
	
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3304.a
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				OR = {
					has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
					has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 3 }
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 6
			min = 20
			max = 1500
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3304.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				leader = {
					leader_class = ruler
					OR = {
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
					}
				}
			}
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3304.success
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = ruler_teaching_to_play
			days = 3600
		}
		event_target:ruler = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = leader_trait_nervous
				}
				remove_trait = leader_trait_nervous
				add_trait = trait_ruler_deep_connections
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 1 }
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 350
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3304.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				leader = {
					leader_class = ruler
					OR = {
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_psionic
						has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_chosen
					}
				}
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3304.success
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				subtract_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value = 5 }
			}
		}
		add_influence = -25
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.hobby.exp.decrease.tooltip
	}
	after = {
	}
}

#GET A NEW TRAIT AND REMOVE THE OLD ONE
country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3310
	title = play_as_ruler.3310.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3310.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_galactic_senate
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
#	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	location = event_target:planet

	trigger = {	
		has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_has_hobby_event
		influence > 100
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler			
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			or = {
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict_experienced		
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_edict_expert
			}
			check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value > 15 }
			NOT = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_cooldown
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.3310_event_cooldown
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1080
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			effect_play_as_ruler_hobby_event_ended = yes
		}
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			set_timed_leader_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler.3310_event_cooldown days = 3600 }
		}
		random_owned_planet = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = planet
		}
		country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3311 }
	}
	after = {
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3313
	title = play_as_ruler.3313.name
#	desc = play_as_ruler.3313.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_galactic_senate
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes
	location = event_target:planet

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			success_text = { 
				text = play_as_ruler.3313.desc_bad
				event_target:ruler = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_fail
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3313.desc_ok
				event_target:ruler = {
					NOT = {
						has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_fail
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {	
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 1080
#	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_fail
				}	
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_ok1
				}
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_corvette_focus
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_ok2
				}
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_destroyer_focus
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_ok3
				}
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_cruiser_focus
			}

				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_ok4
				}
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_battleship_focus
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_ok5
				}
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_recruiter
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_ok6
				}
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_fortifier
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_ok7
				}
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_logistic_understanding
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_ok8
				}
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_military_pioneer
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_ok9
				}
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_warlike
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_ok10
				}
				remove_trait = trait_ruler_architectural_sense

	option = {
		name = UNFORTUNATE
		trigger = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_fail
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				subtract_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value = 10 }
			}
		}
		add_influence = -25
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.hobby.exp.decrease.tooltip
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		trigger = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				NOT = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_fail			
				}
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 350
		}
	}
	after = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
				NOT = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_remove_trait_fail
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 1 }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_corvette_focus }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_destroyer_focus }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_cruiser_focus }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_battleship_focus }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_recruiter }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_fortifier }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_logistic_understanding }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_military_pioneer }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_warlike }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_architectural_sense }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_frontier_spirit }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_world_shaper }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_home_in_the_sky }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_industrialist }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_eye_for_talent }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_deep_connections }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_charismatic }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_champion_of_the_people }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_expansionist }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_fertility_preacher }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_investor }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_space_miner }
					1 = { add_trait = trait_ruler_explorer }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_fleet_organizer }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_reformer }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3400
	title = play_as_ruler.3400.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3400.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_researcher
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	is_triggered_only = no
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_has_hobby_event
		influence > 125
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			or = {
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_research_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_physic_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_social_expert
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_engineering_expert
			}
			check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value > 15 }
			NOT = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_cooldown
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.3400_event_cooldown
			}
		}
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = scientist
			OR = {
				is_researching_area = physics
				is_researching_area = society
				is_researching_area = engineering
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1080
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			effect_play_as_ruler_hobby_event_ended = yes
		}
		random_list = {
			1 = { set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_physics }
			1 = { set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_society }
			1 = { set_country_flag = play_as_ruler_engineering }
		}
		event_target:ruler = {
			set_timed_leader_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler.3400_event_cooldown days = 3600 }
		}
		every_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = scientist
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_researching_area = physics
				}
				save_event_target_as = scientist1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_researching_area = society
				}
				save_event_target_as = scientist2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_researching_area = engineering
				}
				save_event_target_as = scientist3
			}
		}	
		country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3401 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3401
	title = play_as_ruler.3400.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3401.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_researcher
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	is_triggered_only = yes
#	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {	

	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = scientist
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_researching_area = physics
				}
				save_event_target_as = scientist1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_researching_area = society
				}
				save_event_target_as = scientist2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_researching_area = engineering
				}
				save_event_target_as = scientist3
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3401.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_physics
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				70 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3402 days = 20 random = 20 } }
				30 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3403 days = 20 random = 20 } }
			}
			event_target:scientist1 = {
				set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.3400.target
			}
		}
		add_influence = -25
	}

	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3401.b

					has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3400.diy
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3402.desc_02		
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3400.diy
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {

				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}

		}
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = scientist

			}

			max = 40
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 350
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = society_research
			value = 12
			min = 120
			max = 2500
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler_engineering
			NOT = {

		}

			max = 350
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = engineering_research
			value = 12

			max = 2500
		}

		trigger = {

		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = influence
			value = 3

			max = 40
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 350
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = physics_research
			value = 4
			min = 60
			max = 1000
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = society_research
			value = 4
			min = 60
			max = 1000
		}
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = engineering_research
			value = 4
			min = 60
			max = 1000
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 3 }
			}
			event_target:scientist = {
				remove_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.3400.target
			}
		}
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_physics
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_society
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler_engineering
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3900
	title = play_as_ruler.3900.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3900.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_investor
	show_sound = event_administrative_work
	location = event_target:planet
	is_triggered_only = no

	trigger = {	
		has_country_edict = play_as_ruler_has_hobby_event
		energy > 1000
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value > 15 }
			or = {
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_expert
			}
			NOT = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_cooldown
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.3900_event_cooldown
			}
		}
		any_owned_planet = {
			exists = leader
			leader = {
				leader_class = governor
			}
			num_pops > 1
			has_ground_combat = no
			num_energy > 6
			NOT = {
				has_planet_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.planet_event
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1080
	}
	
	immediate = {
		effect_play_as_ruler_hobby_event_ended = yes
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			save_event_target_as = ruler
			set_timed_leader_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler.3900_event_cooldown days = 3600 }
		}
		random_owned_planet = {
			limit = {
				exists = leader
				leader = {
					leader_class = governor
				}
				NOT = {
					has_planet_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.planet_event
				}
				num_pops > 1
				has_ground_combat = no
				num_energy > 6
			}
			leader = {
				set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.governor
			}
			save_event_target_as = planet
			set_planet_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.planet
			set_planet_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.planet_event
		}
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.governor
			}
			save_event_target_as = governor
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3900.a
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
			}
			OR = {
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_expert
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3901 days = 30 random = 60 }
		}
		set_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.high
		add_energy = -1000
	}
	
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3900.a
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.hobby.exp.highenough.tooltip
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_experienced
				has_trait = trait_ruler_hobby_investor_expert
			}
			check_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value > 30 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3901 days = 30 random = 60 }
			subtract_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_hobby_exp value = 20 }
		}
		set_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.high
		add_energy = -1000
	}

	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3900.b
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3901 days = 30 random = 60 } }
				50 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3902 days = 30 random = 60 } }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.high
		add_energy = -1000
	}
	
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3900.c
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3901 days = 30 random = 60 } }
				50 = { country_event = { id = play_as_ruler.3902 days = 30 random = 60 } }
			}
		}
		add_energy = -250
	}
	
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.3900.d
		event_target:planet = {
			remove_planet_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.planet
			remove_planet_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.planet_event
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.3901
	title = play_as_ruler.3901.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.3901.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_hobby_investor
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
	location = event_target:planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	desc = {
		trigger = {		
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3901.desc_high
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.high 
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {		
			success_text = {
				text = play_as_ruler.3901.desc_low
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.high
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {	
	}

#	mean_time_to_happen = {
#		days = 1080
#	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			save_event_target_as = ruler
		}
		random_owned_planet = {
			limit = {
				exists = leader
				leader = {
					leader_class = governor
				}
				has_planet_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.planet
			}
			save_event_target_as = planet
		}
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.governor
			}
			save_event_target_as = governor
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.high
		}
		event_target:planet = {
			random_tile = {
				limit = {
					has_resource = { type = energy amount > 0 }
				}
				add_deposit = d_rich_energy_deposit
			}
			random_tile = {
				limit = {
					has_resource = { type = energy amount > 0 }
				}
				add_deposit = d_rich_energy_deposit
			}
			random_tile = {
				limit = {
					has_resource = { type = energy amount > 0 }
				}
				add_deposit = d_rich_energy_deposit
			}
			random_tile = {
				limit = {
					has_resource = { type = energy amount > 0 }
				}
				add_deposit = d_energy_deposit
			}
			random_tile = {
				limit = {
					has_resource = { type = energy amount > 0 }
				}
				add_deposit = d_energy_deposit
			}
		}
		event_target:governor = {
			add_experience = 350
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_trait = leader_trait_architectural_interest
					}
				}
				add_trait = leader_trait_architectural_interest
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = influence
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 40
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 350
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.hobby.reward.good_01
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.high			
			}
		}
		event_target:planet = {
			random_tile = {
				limit = {
					has_resource = { type = energy amount > 0 }
				}
				add_deposit = d_energy_deposit
			}
			random_tile = {
				limit = {
					has_resource = { type = energy amount > 0 }
				}
				add_deposit = d_energy_deposit
			}
			random_tile = {
				limit = {
					has_resource = { type = energy amount > 0 }
				}
				add_deposit = d_energy_deposit
			}
		}
		event_target:governor = {
			add_experience = 200
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = influence
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 40
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = 3
			min = 20
			max = 350
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ruler = {
				change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		event_target:governor = {
			remove_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.governor
		}
		event_target:planet = {
			remove_planet_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.planet
		}
		remove_country_flag = play_as_ruler.3900.high
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.4500
	title = play_as_ruler.4500.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.4500.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_psionics
	show_sound = event_psionic
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_modifier = shroud_cooldown
			has_modifier = shroud_precog_cooldown
		}
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			NOT = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler.4500_event_cooldown
			}			
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7200
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			any_owned_leader = {
				has_trait =	leader_trait_ruler_psionic 
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			any_owned_leader = {
				has_trait =	leader_trait_ruler_chosen 
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		remove_modifier = shroud_cooldown
		remove_modifier = shroud_precog_cooldown
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
			set_timed_leader_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler.4500_event_cooldown days = 3600 }
			save_event_target_as = ruler
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = play_as_ruler.4500.a
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				or = {
					has_trait =	leader_trait_ruler_psionic	
					has_trait =	leader_trait_ruler_chosen					
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.4500.tooltip
	}
	option = {
		name = GOOD
		trigger = {
			leader = {
				leader_class = ruler
				NOR = {
					has_trait =	leader_trait_ruler_psionic
					has_trait =	leader_trait_ruler_chosen
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = play_as_ruler.4500.tooltip		
	}
	after = {
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = play_as_ruler.10000
	title = play_as_ruler.10000.name
	desc = play_as_ruler.10000.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ruler_title
	show_sound = event_Building_Completed
#	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {	
		any_owned_leader = {
			leader_class = ruler
			OR = {
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv1
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv2
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv3
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv4
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv5
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv6
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv7
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv8
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv9
				has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv10
			}
			NOT = {
				has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				leader_class = ruler
				OR = {
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv1
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv2
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv3
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv4
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv5
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv6
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv7
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv8
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv9
					has_trait = trait_witness_ruler_lv10				
				}
				NOT = {
					has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
				}			
			}
			set_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
		}
	}
